    <div

        <div class="wiki-block-inner">
            <div class="
                wiki-block-inner-2
                
                    wiki-truncate-4-lines
                
            ">
                
                <a href="/music/Loaded">Loaded</a> (also known as <a href="/music/Duff+McKagan's+Loaded">Duff McKagan&#x27;s Loaded</a>) is an American <a href="/tag/hard+rock" rel="tag">hard rock</a> <a href="/tag/supergroup" rel="tag">supergroup</a> that formed in Seattle, Washington in 1999. It&#x27;s current lineup consists of founder <a href="/music/Duff+McKagan">Duff McKagan</a> of <a href="/music/Velvet+Revolver">Velvet Revolver</a>, formerly of <a href="/music/Guns+N'+Roses">Guns N&#x27; Roses</a>, on lead vocals and guitar, <a href="/music/Mike+Squires">Mike Squires</a> formerly of <a href="/music/Alien+Crime+Syndicate">Alien Crime Syndicate</a> and <a href="/music/Nevada+Bachelors">Nevada Bachelors</a> on lead guitar, <a href="/music/Jeff+Rouse">Jeff Rouse</a> formerly of <a href="/music/Alien+Crime+Syndicate">Alien Crime Syndicate</a>, <a href="/music/Vendetta+Red">Vendetta Red</a>, and <a href="/music/Sirens+Sister">Sirens Sister</a> on bass and drummer <a href="/music/Isaac+Carpenter">Isaac Carpenter</a> formerly of <a href="/music/Loudermilk">Loudermilk</a>, <a href="/music/Gosling">Gosling</a> and <a href="/music/The+Exies">The Exies</a>. They have released two albums (<a href="/music/Loaded/Dark+Days">Dark Days</a> and <a href="/music/Duff+McKagan's+Loaded/Sick">Sick</a>) one EP (<a href="/music/Duff+McKagan's+Loaded/Wasted+Heart">Wasted Heart</a>) and  <a href="/music/Duff+McKagan%27s+Loaded/+wiki">read more</a>
